Convert the list of tuples to a dict for easier checking\n    settings_dict = dict(dark_mode_settings_list)\n\n    # Check that the correct Chromium setting name is present\n    # For Qt 6.4, it should be 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', NOT 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\n    assert 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' in settings_dict, (\n        f\"Expected 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for Qt 6.4 dark-mode-settings, \"\n        f\"but got: {settings_dict}. \"\n        f\"The threshold.text setting is using the old Chromium setting name \"\n        f\"(TextBrightnessThreshold) which was renamed in Chromium 99.0.4785.0. \"\n        f\"Qt 6.4 requires the new name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'.\"\n    )\n    assert settings_dict['ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'] == '100'\n\n    # This test verifies that qutebrowser\n    generates the correct setting name for the dark-mode-settings switch.\n\n    This test FAILS on the buggy code (which still uses TextBrightnessThreshold\n    for Qt 6.4) and will PASS once the fix is applied (which introduces a\n    separate Variant.qt_64 that uses ForegroundBrightnessThreshold).\n    \"\"\"\n    # issue.\n\nBug Description:\nWhen users configure the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) on Qt 6.4+, the setting has no\neffect because the Chromium setting name changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold`\nto `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold` in Chromium 99.0.4785.0.\n\nThis test verifies that the correct Chromium setting name is used for each\nQt version.\n\nRun with: python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null regression_test.py -v\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Ensure the /app directory is in the Python path\nif '/app' not in sys.path:\n Qt 6.4 uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.\n\n    On Qt 6.4 and later, Chromium renamed TextBrightnessThreshold to\n    ForegroundBrightnessThreshold. This test verifies that qutebrowser\n    generates the correct setting name for the dark-mode-settings switch.\n\n    This test FAILS on the buggy code (which still uses TextBrightnessThreshold\n    for Qt 6.4) and will PASS once the fix is applied (which introduces a\n    separate Variant.qt_64 that uses ForegroundBrightnessThreshold).\n    \"\"\"\n    # Configure dark mode with a custom text threshold value\n    config_stub.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled = True\n    config_stub.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.algorithm = 'brightness-rgb'\n    config_stub.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text', 100)\n\n    # Get settings for Qt 6.4\n    versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n    darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n    # Extract the dark-mode-settings (not blink-settings)\n    dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n    # Convert the list of tuples to a dict for easier checking\n    settings_dict = dict(dark_mode_settings_list)\n\n    # Check that the correct Chromium setting name is present\n    # For Qt 6.4, it should be 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', NOT 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\n    assert 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' in settings_dict, (\n        f\"Expected 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for Qt 6.4 dark-mode-settings, \"\n        f\"but got: {settings_dict}. \"\n        f\"The threshold.text setting is using the old Chromium setting name \"\n        f\"(TextBrightnessThreshold) which was renamed in Chromium 99.0.4785.0. \"\n        f\"Qt 6.4 requires the new name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'.\"\n    )\n    assert settings_dict['ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'] == '100'\n\n    # Make sure the old name is NOT present\n    assert 'TextBrightnessThreshold' not in settings_dict, (\n        f\"Found old Chromium setting name 'TextBrightnessThreshold' in Qt 6.4 settings. \"\n        f\"This was renamed to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' in Chromium 99.0.4785.0. \"\n        f\"Full settings: {settings_dict}\"\n    )\n\n\ndef test_qt63_still_uses_text_brightness_threshold(config_stub):\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.3 still uses TextBrightnessThreshold.\n\n    Qt 6.3 uses the old Chromium setting name, so this test verifies that\n    the fix doesn't break Qt 6.3 compatibility.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Configure dark mode with a custom text threshold value\n    config_stub.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled = True\n    config_stub.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.algorithm = 'brightness-rgb'\n    config_stub.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text', 150)\n\n    # no\neffect because the Chromium setting name changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold`\nto `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold` in Chromium 99.0.4785.0.\n\nThis test demonstrates the bug and verifies the Chromium setting name for text threshold.\n\n    On Qt 6.4 and later, Chromium renamed TextBrightnessThreshold to\n    ForegroundBrightnessThreshold. This test verifies that qutebrowser\n    generates the correct setting name for the dark-mode-settings switch.\n\n    This test FAILS on the buggy code (which still uses TextBrightnessThreshold\n    for Qt 6.4) and will PASS once the fix is applied (which introduces a\n    separate Variant.qt_64 that uses ForegroundBrightnessThreshold).\n    \"\"\"\n    #
